INNER JOIN [Personeller] AS [p] ON [t].[PersonelId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[Id], [t1].[AdliyeId], [t1].[Sira], [t1].[TayinTalepId], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[Ad]
    FROM [TayinTalepTercihleri] AS [t1]
    INNER JOIN [Adliyeler] AS [a] ON [t1].[AdliyeId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[TayinTalepId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [p].[Id], [t0].[Id]
